2147	def test_supports() -> None:
2148	    """
2149	    Test ``supports``.
2150	
2151	    The method should use the catalog, in addition to validating the URLs.
2152	    """
2153	    assert GSheetsAPI.supports("https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1/edit")
2154	    assert not GSheetsAPI.supports("https://github.com/betodealmeida/shillelagh/")
2155	
2156	    assert not GSheetsAPI.supports("some_table")
2157	    assert GSheetsAPI.supports(
2158	        "some_table",
2159	        catalog={"some_table": "https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1/edit"},
2160	    )
2161	    assert not GSheetsAPI.supports(
2162	        "some_table",
2163	        catalog={"some_table": "https://github.com/betodealmeida/shillelagh/"},
2164	    )
2165
